	 	  //guanggao
          function daohang_adHtml(json){
            var htmls="";
              if(json != ""){ 
                   htmls +='<li>';
                    htmls +='     <a href="'+json.url+'" target="_blank">';
                    htmls +='       <img class="min_img" src="'+json.pic+'?imageView2/1/w/250/h/50">';
                    htmls +='     </a><div class="big_img">';
                    htmls +='       <a href="'+json.url+'" target="_blank">';
                      if(json.pic2 !=""){
                        htmls +='     <img  src="'+json.pic2+'?imageView2/1/w/500/h/180" width="500px" height="180px">';
                      }
                    htmls +='    </a></div> ';
                    htmls +='</li>';
                $(".nav-guanggao").html(htmls);    
              }
            }  
 
          function getTopHtml(json,index){
              var htmls="";
                for( var i in json ){
                    htmls +='<li>';
                    htmls +='    <a href="'+json[i].url+'" class="img" target="_blank">';
                    htmls +='       <img  src="'+json[i].picture+'?imageView2/1/w/152/h/87" width="152px" height="87px" alt="" />';
                    htmls +='       <div class="describe">'+json[i].title+'</div>';
                    htmls +='     </a>';
                    htmls +='</li>';
                }
                $("#"+index+"").html(htmls);    
          }  
          function getTopHtml2(json,index){
              var htmls="";
                for( var i in json ){
                    htmls +='<li>';
                    htmls +='   <a href="'+json[i].url+'" class="img" target="_blank"><img style="border-radius: 16px;" src="'+json[i].icon+'?imageView2/1/w/90/h/90" width="90px" height="90px" alt="">';
                    htmls +='     <div class="name">'+json[i].name+'</div>';
                 	if(typeof(json[i].time) !="undefined"){
                       htmls +='     <div class="time">'+json[i].time +'</div>';
                    }else{
                      htmls +='     <div class="time"></div>';
                    }
                    htmls +='   </a>';
                    htmls +='</li>'; 
                }
                $("#"+index+"").html(htmls);    
          }  
         function getTopHtml3(json,index){
                      var htmls="";
                        for( var i in json ){
                            htmls +='<li>';
                            htmls +='    <a href="'+json[i].url+'" class="img" target="_blank">';
                            htmls +='       <img  src="'+json[i].picture+'?imageView2/1/w/152/h/87" width="152px" height="87px" alt="" />';
                            htmls +='       <div class="describe">'+json[i].name+'</div>';
                            htmls +='     </a>';
                            htmls +='</li>';
                        }
                        $("#"+index+"").html(htmls);    
                  }  
		
		//广告
		$(".mainNav .nav-guanggao").mouseover(function(){
            $(".mainNav .nav-guanggao .big_img").show();
          }).mouseout(function(){
            $(".mainNav .nav-guanggao .big_img").hide();
          });

          //bg
          $(".mainNav .nav-hover .first-nav").mouseover(function(event){
              $(".mainNav .bg").css({"display":"block","border-bottom":"2px solid rgb(250,188,80)","height":"220px","padding":"30px 0;"});
              event.preventDefault();
          }).mouseout(function(){
              $(".mainNav .bg").css({"height":"0","border-bottom":"0 solid rgb(231,231,231)"});
              event.preventDefault();
            
          });

          //二级切换
          $(".mainNav .navbar_subnav .second-tab .second-tab-content").mouseover(function(event){
                var index = $(this).index();
      
               $(this).parents(".navbar_subnav").find(".second-tab-content").removeClass("active");
               $(this).parents(".navbar_subnav").find('.second-tab-content:eq('+index+')').addClass('active');
                //console.log(index);
                $(this).parents(".navbar_subnav").find(".hb .content").removeClass("active");
                //$(".navbar_subnav .hb .content").removeClass("active");
                $(this).parents(".navbar_subnav").find('.hb .content:eq('+index+')').addClass('active');
           }); 
		
		
    });
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(function(){
        $("#ce-index").on("click",".ce-Nav li",function(){
            $(".ce-Nav li").removeClass("active");
            $(this).addClass("active");
        });

        $(".showewm").on("click",function(){
            var parent = $(this).parent();
            if(parent.hasClass("show")){
                parent.removeClass("show");
            }
            else{
                parent.addClass("show");
            }
        });
    })
  </script>
